The following two major patterns can be distinguished:
<ul style="list-style-type:disc"><li><p>the power level at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-196-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-196">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> approaches the power level at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-197-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-197">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> as the input voltage to the rectifier <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">V_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-198-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-198">V_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> increases;</p></li><li><p>the power level at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-199-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-199">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> approaches the power level at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-200-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-200">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> as <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-201-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-201">Q</script></tex-math></inline-formula> decreases.</p></li></ul>It is expected that with higher <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-202-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-202">Q</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, the rectifier input voltage at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-203-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-203">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is also higher, leading to a greater nonlinear effect, and therefore causing the rectifier to produce a higher component at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-204-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-204">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. However, a higher <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-205-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-205">Q</script></tex-math></inline-formula> also ensures a higher attenuation at frequencies different than <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-206-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-206">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. Summarizing, when higher is <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-207-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-207">Q</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, higher is the suppression of the power transmitted from the chip to its antenna at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-208-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-208">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>.<p></p><p>
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig8"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7234979/7166335/7166335-fig-8-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7234979/7166335/7166335-fig-8-small.gif" alt="Figure 8" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 8. </b><fig><p>Law decay of the power at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-209-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-209">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> with respect to the power at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-210-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-210">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> in function of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-211-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-211">Q</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">V_{0}/V_{t}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-212-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-212">V_{0}/V_{t}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> for traditional tags.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7166335/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
The harmonic power can be potentially radiated if the antenna structure allows it, i.e., profiting from the current distribution of harmonics in a specific antenna structure <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref27" id="context_ref_27_2b2">[27]</a>. According to the exposed model, a traditional RFID tag having a dipole antenna structure, which has a current distribution at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-213-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-213">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> different than zero at the input and a distributed matching network with, for instance, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q=4</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-214-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-214">Q=4</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, radiates a signal at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-215-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-215">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, being 22.3 dB lower than the signal at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-216-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-216">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. This model explains why certain commercial tags backscatter a signal at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-217-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-217">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> with stronger level than others, certainly depending on the tag antenna structure, as evidenced in <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref27" id="context_ref_27_2b2">[27]</a> for the tag Rafsec MemoryStick <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref44" id="context_ref_44_2b2">[44]</a> (note that this tag will be used as comparative reference in the performance tests in <a ref-type="sec" anchor="sec4" class="fulltext-link">Section IV</a>).<p></p></div></div><div class="section_2" id="sec2c"><h3>C. Third Harmonic Enhancement in New Harmonic Tag Antennas</h3><div class="section_2" id="sec2c1"><h4>1. Dual-Band Impedance-Matching Network</h4><p>A new matching network model that could enhance the backscattering strength of HTs at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-218-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-218">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is presented in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig9" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 9</a>. The model is based on the previous one presented in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig7" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 7</a> to explain the operation of the HT at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-219-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-219">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The new matching network composed by the cascading of two <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">LC</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-220-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-220">LC</script></tex-math></inline-formula> networks is characterized by a new quality factor <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q^{\ast}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-221-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-221">Q^{\ast}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> calculated as <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref45" id="context_ref_45_2c1">[45]</a>, <disp-formula id="deqn16" class="display-formula"><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q^{\ast}=\sqrt{\left({R_{\rm eq}\over R_{A}}\right)^{1\over 2}-1}.\eqno{\hbox{(16)}}</span><div class="MathJax_Display MathJax_Processing"><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-222-Frame" tabindex="0"></span></div><script type="math/tex; mode=display" id="MathJax-Element-222">Q^{\ast}=\sqrt{\left({R_{\rm eq}\over R_{A}}\right)^{1\over 2}-1}.\eqno{\hbox{(16)}}</script></tex-math><span class="formula"><span class="link">View Source</span><img aria-describedby="qtip-0" style="display:inline;" title="Right-click on figure or equation for MathML and additional features." data-hasqtip="0" class="qtooltip moreInfo" alt="Right-click on figure for MathML and additional features." src="/assets/img/icon.support.gif" border="0" height="20" width="24" /><span class="tex tex2jax_ignore" style="display:none;">Q^{\ast}=\sqrt{\left({R_{\rm eq}\over R_{A}}\right)^{1\over 2}-1}.\eqno{\hbox{(16)}}</span></span></disp-formula>It is worth noting that in this case the calculation of <a ref-type="disp-formula" anchor="deqn16" href="#deqn16" class="fulltext-link">(16)</a> considers the lowest <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">Q^{\ast}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-223-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-223">Q^{\ast}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> achievable in benefit of a greater bandwidth at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-224-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-224">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>.
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig9"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7234979/7166335/7166335-fig-9-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7234979/7166335/7166335-fig-9-small.gif" alt="Figure 9" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 9. </b><fig><p>Proposed matching network to exploit the signal generated by the RFID chip at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-225-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-225">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The cascade <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">LC</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-226-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-226">LC</script></tex-math></inline-formula> matching network allows the chip to transmit a maximum power towards the antenna at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-227-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-227">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>; <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L^{\prime}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-228-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-228">L^{\prime}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> always being considered in the analysis.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7166335/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
<p></p><p>The new element introduced is the series inductance <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-229-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-229">L_{3f}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> that resonates with both, the original <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">LC</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-230-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-230">LC</script></tex-math></inline-formula> network and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">C_{\rm eq}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-231-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-231">C_{\rm eq}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-232-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-232">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The new matching network should be dimensioned choosing an <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-233-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-233">L_{3f}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, which does not affect the operation at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-234-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-234">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, i.e., <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-235-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-235">L_{3f}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> should act as a short circuit at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-236-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-236">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. In the same way, the dimensioning criterion has to consider that the shunt inductance <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L^{\prime}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-237-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-237">L^{\prime}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> should not intervene in the operation at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-238-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-238">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, i.e., <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L^{\prime}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-239-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-239">L^{\prime}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> should act as an open circuit at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-240-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-240">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The first step to choose the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-241-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-241">L_{3f}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> value is to calculate the inductance necessary to compensate the chip capacitance at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-242-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-242">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> (inductive matching), and depending on the values of the original <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">LC</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-243-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-243">LC</script></tex-math></inline-formula> network, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-244-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-244">L_{3f}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> should be tuned to resonate at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-245-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-245">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. Realistic values for the proposed model are <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">C_{\rm eq}=1.03\ {\hbox{pF}}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-246-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-246">C_{\rm eq}=1.03\ {\hbox{pF}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">R_{\rm eq}=1.70\ {\hbox{k}}\Omega</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-247-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-247">R_{\rm eq}=1.70\ {\hbox{k}}\Omega</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L^{\prime}=32.90\ {\hbox{nH}}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-248-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-248">L^{\prime}=32.90\ {\hbox{nH}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">L_{3f}=11.11\ {\hbox{nH}}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-249-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-249">L_{3f}=11.11\ {\hbox{nH}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">C=0.60\ {\hbox{pF}}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-250-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">R_{A}=61.70\ \Omega</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-252-Frame" shows the transmission coefficient of the proposed matching network for the HT compared to the matching network of a traditional tag. It can be seen that the resonance at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-253-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-253">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> coexists with the one at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-254-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-254">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, a fact that will lead to the dual-band operation of the HT.

ref-type="disp-formula" anchor="deqn14-15" href="#deqn14-15" class="fulltext-link">(14)</a> and <a ref-type="disp-formula" anchor="deqn14-15" href="#deqn14-15" class="fulltext-link">(15)</a>, respectively, the power radiated by the HT at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-270-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-270">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-271-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-271">3f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> can be expressed as <disp-formula id="deqn20-21" class="display-formula"><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">\eqalignno{P_{\rm 1HT}=&amp;\,{I_{10}^{2}(Q^{2}+1)R_{A}\over 2}&amp;\hbox{(20)}\cr P_{\rm 3HT}=&amp;\,{I_{30}^{2}(Q^{2}+1)R_{A}\over 2}.&amp;\hbox{(21)}}</span><div class="MathJax_Display MathJax_Processing"><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-272-Frame" tabindex="0"></span></div><script type="math/tex; mode=display" id="MathJax-Element-272">\eqalignno{P_{\rm 1HT}=&amp;\,{I_{10}^{2}(Q^{2}+1)R_{A}\over 2}&amp;\hbox{(20)}\cr P_{\rm 3HT}=&amp;\,{I_{30}^{2}(Q^{2}+1)R_{A}\over 2}.&amp;\hbox{(21)}}</script></tex-math><span class="formula"><span class="link">View Source</span><img aria-describedby="qtip-0" style="display:inline;" title="Right-click on figure or equation for 2}.&amp;\hbox{(21)}}</span></span></disp-formula> <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig11" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 11(a)</a> represents the law decay of the power <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">P_{\rm 3HT}</span><span class="MathJax MathJax_Processing" id="MathJax-Element-273-Frame" tabindex="0"></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-273">P_{\rm 3HT}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview">3f_{0}</span><span class="MathJax
